Kegiatan Pemanfaatan Ruang (PKKPR) Berusaha</a><div class="modal fade" id="modal-info-215" tabindex="-1" role="dialog"><div class="modal-dialog"><div class="modal-content"><div class="modal-header"><h5 class="modal-title">Persetujuan Kesesuaian Kegiatan Pemanfaatan Ruang (PKKPR) Berusaha</h5><button type="button" class="close" data-dismiss="modal"><span>&times;</span></button></div><div class="modal-body"><p><span style="font-weight: bold;">Alur Pengajuan&nbsp;</span></p>


<ol><li>Permohonan PKKPR Berusaha melalui oss.go.id</li>
	<li>UKM - Pernyataaan Mandiri - Kajian Teknis Tata Ruang (KTTR)&nbsp;</li>
	<li>Non UKM&nbsp;</li>
</ol>


<p><span style="font-weight: bold;">Proses&nbsp;</span></p>


<ul><li>Validasi<br />
	</li>
	<li>Pertimbangan Teknis Pertanahan (PTP/Pertek) BPN<br />
	</li>
	<li>Survey &amp; Pemetaan<br />
	</li>
	<li>Rapat Pembahasan PKKPR Berusaha<br />
	</li>
	<li>Kajian Forum Penataan Ruang (FPR)<br />
	</li>
	<li>Penerbitan PKKPR Berusaha<br />
	</li>
</ul>


<p><span style="font-weight: bold;">Persyaratan Pengajuan Layanan</span></p>


<ul><li>Menyertakan hasil Validasi Sertipikat yang dimohonkan dari BPN<br />
	</li>
	<li>Upload SHP sesuai luasan yang diajukan<br />
	</li>
	<li>Upload Sertifikat SHM (Jika Hak Milik Sendiri), Upload Surat Sewa yang diketahui Notaris Resmi bertanda tangan diatas Materai (Jika Sewa), Upload Dokumen Pendukung Perizinan Kegiatan (Akta Pendirian Perusahaan, dll)<br />
	</li>
	<li>Menyertakan Dokumen NIB dan KBLI dari OSS sesuai lokasi kegiatan yang dimohonkan<br />
	</li>
	<li>Upload Rencana Teknis Bangunan (Siteplan Rencana Bangunan) disertakan penjabaran luasan masing-masing ruangan yang dituangkan kedalam kolom keterangan dan perhitungan Ruang Terbuka Hijau (RTH)</li>
</ul>


<p><br /></p>

<script>
function checkIsMobile() {
    return window.innerWidth <= 991.98;
}

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
    document.querySelectorAll('.tooltip-wrapper').forEach(function(wrapper) {
        wrapper.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
            if (!checkIsMobile()) return;

            const isLink = e.target.tagName.toLowerCase() === 'a';
            if (isLink) return;

            e.preventDefault();
            e.stopPropagation();

            const wasActive = wrapper.classList.contains('active');
            document.querySelectorAll('.tooltip-wrapper').forEach(w => w.classList.remove('active'));
            document.body.classList.remove('no-scroll');

            if (!wasActive) {
                wrapper.classList.add('active');
                // document.body.classList.add('no-scroll');
                lastScrollTop = window.scrollY || document.documentElement.scrollTop;
                document.body.classList.add('no-scroll');
                document.body.style.top = `-${lastScrollTop}px`;


                const tooltip = wrapper.querySelector('.tooltip-submenu');
                if (tooltip && !tooltip.querySelector('.close-tooltip')) {
                    const header = document.createElement('div');
                    header.classList.add('submenu-header');

                    const title = document.createElement('div');
                    title.classList.add('title');
                    title.textContent = wrapper.querySelector('.fw-bold')?.innerText || 'Submenu';

                    const closeBtn = document.createElement('div');
                    closeBtn.classList.add('close-tooltip');
                    closeBtn.innerHTML = '&times;';

                    header.appendChild(title);
                    header.appendChild(closeBtn);
                    tooltip.prepend(header);

                    closeBtn.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
                        e.stopPropagation();
                        wrapper.classList.remove('active');
                        document.body.classList.remove('no-scroll');
                        document.body.style.top = '';
                        window.scrollTo(0, lastScrollTop);

                    });
                }
            }
        });

        wrapper.addEventListener('mouseenter', function () {
            if (checkIsMobile()) return;

            const tooltip = wrapper.querySelector('.tooltip-submenu');
            if (!tooltip) return;

            tooltip.classList.remove('left');

            const rect = tooltip.getBoundingClientRect();
            const overflowsRight = rect.right > window.innerWidth;

            if (overflowsRight) {
                tooltip.classList.add('left');
            }
        });
    });

    document.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
        if (checkIsMobile() && !e.target.closest('.tooltip-wrapper')) {
            document.querySelectorAll('.tooltip-wrapper').forEach(w => w.classList.remove('active'));
            document.body.classList.remove('no-scroll');
        }
    });

    window.addEventListener('resize', function () {
        document.querySelectorAll('.tooltip-wrapper').forEach(w => w.classList.remove('active'));
        document.body.classList.remove('no-scroll');
    });
});

// MOdal
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
    // Simpan posisi scroll sebelum modal dibuka
    let lastScrollTop = 0;

    $('.modal').on('show.bs.modal', function () {
        lastScrollTop = window.pageYOffset || document.documentElement.scrollTop;
    });

    $('.modal').on('hidden.bs.modal', function () {
        window.scrollTo(0, lastScrollTop);
    });
});

</script>
<script>
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
    let lastScrollTop = 0;
    let lastTooltipWrapper = null;

    // Saat modal info dibuka
    $('.modal').on('show.bs.modal', function () {
        lastScrollTop = window.pageYOffset || document.documentElement.scrollTop;
        lastTooltipWrapper = document.querySelector('.tooltip-wrapper.active');
    });

    // Saat modal info ditutup
    $('.modal').on('hidden.bs.modal', function () {
        // Scroll balik ke posisi sebelumnya
        window.scrollTo(0, lastScrollTop);

        // Tampilkan kembali tooltip submenu terakhir jika di mobile
        if (window.innerWidth <= 991.98 && lastTooltipWrapper) {
            // Delay sedikit supaya modal benar-benar tertutup
            setTimeout(() => {
                lastTooltipWrapper.classList.add('active');
            }, 200);
        }
    });
});
</script>

     $(document).ready(function() {
        $('.item-link').on('click', function() {
            const id = $(this).data('id');

                url: `/tautan/${id}`,
                method: "GET",

                error: function(xhr) {
                    // Tangani error

            });

    <!-- Script -->

    <script>
        var geoJson = ""
        var sLayerGroup = new L.LayerGroup();
        var osmUrl = 'http://{s}.tile.openstreetmap.org/{z}/{x}/{y}.png',
            osmAttrib = '&copy; <a href="http://openstreetmap.org/copyright">OpenStreetMap</a> contributors',
            osm = L.tileLayer(osmUrl, {
                maxZoom: 18,
                attribution: osmAttrib
            }),
            map = new L.Map('map', {
                center: new L.LatLng(-6.830020345295199, 110.83360033020125),
                zoom: 13
            }),
            drawnItems = L.featureGroup().addTo(map);
        L.control.layers({
            'osm': osm.addTo(map),
            "google": L.tileLayer('http://www.google.cn/maps/vt?lyrs=s@189&gl=cn&x={x}&y={y}&z={z}', {
                attribution: 'google'
            })
        }, {
            'drawlayer': drawnItems
        }, {
            position: 'topleft',
            collapsed: false
        }).addTo(map);

        let arr = []
        kudus.features.forEach(element => {
            arr.push(element.properties.name)
        });
        // console.log(arr);
        drawMap(allKudus)

        function drawMap(kudus) {
            geoJson = L.geoJson(kudus).addTo(map);

            // geoJson.clearLayers()
            geoJson.eachLayer(function(layer) {
                layer.bindPopup(layer.feature.properties.name);
            });

            map.fitBounds(geoJson.getBounds());
            // sLayerGroup.removeData();
            sLayerGroup.clearLayers();
            sLayerGroup.addLayer(geoJson);

        }
    </script>
    <script>
        function reMap() {
            map.removeLayer(geoJson)
            drawMap(allKudus)
        }

        function autocomplete(inp, arr) {
            /*the autocomplete function takes two arguments,
            the text field element and an array of possible autocompleted values:*/
            var currentFocus;
            /*execute a function when someone writes in the text field:*/
            inp.addEventListener("input", function(e) {
                var a, b, i, val = this.value;
                /*close any already open lists of autocompleted values*/
                closeAllLists();
                if (!val) {
                    return false;
                }
                currentFocus = -1;
                /*create a DIV element that will contain the items (values):*/
                a = document.createElement("DIV");
                a.setAttribute("id", this.id + "autocomplete-list");
                a.setAttribute("class", "autocomplete-items");
                /*append the DIV element as a child of the autocomplete container:*/
                this.parentNode.appendChild(a);
                /*for each item in the array...*/
                for (i = 0; i < arr.length; i++) {
                    /*check if the item starts with the same letters as the text field value:*/
                    if (arr[i].substr(0, val.length).toUpperCase() == val.toUpperCase()) {
                        /*create a DIV element for each matching element:*/
                        b = document.createElement("DIV");
                        /*make the matching letters bold:*/
                        b.innerHTML = "<strong>" + arr[i].substr(0, val.length) + "</strong>";
                        b.innerHTML += arr[i].substr(val.length);
                        /*insert a input field that will hold the current array item's value:*/
                        b.innerHTML += "<input type='hidden' data-id='" + i + "' data-type4='" + kudus.features[i]
                            .properties.TYPE_4 + "' data-gid4='" + kudus.features[i].properties.GID_4 +
                            "' value='" + arr[i] + "'>";
                        /*execute a function when someone clicks on the item value (DIV element):*/
                        b.addEventListener("click", function(e) {
                            /*insert the value for the autocomplete text field:*/
                            inp.value = this.getElementsByTagName("input")[0].value;
                            // console.log(this.getElementsByTagName("input")[0].getAttribute("data-id"));
                            const type4 = this.getElementsByTagName("input")[0].getAttribute("data-type4");
                            const gid4 = this.getElementsByTagName("input")[0].getAttribute("data-gid4");
                            // let data=
                            // console.log(gid4);
                            if (type4 == "Kecamatan") {
                                showDesa(gid4, "kecamatan")
                            } else {
                                data = {
                                    "type": "FeatureCollection",
                                    "features": [kudus.features[this.getElementsByTagName("input")[0]
                                        .getAttribute("data-id")]]
                                }
                            }

                            // $(`.desc-show`).css("display","none")
                            // console.log(`#a-${gid4}`);
                            $(`.show-desc`).css("display", "none")
                            if (document.getElementById(`a-${gid4}`)) {
                                document.getElementById(`a-${gid4}`).style.display = "block"
                            }
                            // console.log($(`#${gid4}`));

                            // console.log(this.getAttribute("data-id"));
                            map.removeLayer(geoJson)
                            drawMap(data)
                            /*close the list of autocompleted values,
                            (or any other open lists of autocompleted values:*/
                            closeAllLists();
                        });
                        a.appendChild(b);
                    }
                }
            });
            /*execute a function presses a key on the keyboard:*/
            inp.addEventListener("keydown", function(e) {
                var x = document.getElementById(this.id + "autocomplete-list");
                if (x) x = x.getElementsByTagName("div");
                if (e.keyCode == 40) {
                    /*If the arrow DOWN key is pressed,
                    increase the currentFocus variable:*/
                    currentFocus++;
                    /*and and make the current item more visible:*/
                    addActive(x);
                } else if (e.keyCode == 38) { //up
                    /*If the arrow UP key is pressed,
                    decrease the currentFocus variable:*/
                    currentFocus--;
                    /*and and make the current item more visible:*/
                    addActive(x);
                } else if (e.keyCode == 13) {
                    /*If the ENTER key is pressed, prevent the form from being submitted,*/
                    e.preventDefault();
                    if (currentFocus > -1) {
                        /*and simulate a click on the "active" item:*/
                        if (x) x[currentFocus].click();
                    }
                }
            });

            function addActive(x) {
                /*a function to classify an item as "active":*/
                if (!x) return false;
                /*start by removing the "active" class on all items:*/
                removeActive(x);
                if (currentFocus >= x.length) currentFocus = 0;
                if (currentFocus < 0) currentFocus = (x.length - 1);
                /*add class "autocomplete-active":*/
                x[currentFocus].classList.add("autocomplete-active");
            }

            function removeActive(x) {
                /*a function to remove the "active" class from all autocomplete items:*/
                for (var i = 0; i < x.length; i++) {
                    x[i].classList.remove("autocomplete-active");
                }
            }

            function closeAllLists(elmnt) {
                /*close all autocomplete lists in the document,
                except the one passed as an argument:*/
                var x = document.getElementsByClassName("autocomplete-items");
                for (var i = 0; i < x.length; i++) {
                    if (elmnt != x[i] && elmnt != inp) {
                        x[i].parentNode.removeChild(x[i]);
                    }
                }
            }
            /*execute a function when someone clicks in the document:*/
            document.addEventListener("click", function(e) {
                closeAllLists(e.target);
            });
        }

        /*An array containing all the country names in the world:*/

        /*initiate the autocomplete function on the "myInput" element, and pass along the countries array as possible autocomplete values:*/
        autocomplete(document.getElementById("myInput"), arr);
    </script>
    <script>
        $(window).on('load', function() {
            $('#loading').hide();
        });

        $(window).on("scroll", function() {
            clearTimeout(this.timer);
            this.timer = setTimeout(() => {
                if (window.innerWidth > 991) {
                    if ($(window).scrollTop() > $('#big-banner').height() / 2) {
                        $('nav.navbar').addClass('bg-blue');
                    } else {
                        $('nav.navbar').removeClass('bg-blue');
                    }
                }
            }, 30);
        });

        $(document).ready(function() {
            // Lazy load images
            $('.lazy').Lazy({
                placeholder: "/assets/images/loader.gif"
            });

            // Header on click menu
            $('.nav-item-top').on('click', function() {
                $('.nav-item-top').not(this).removeClass('menu-active');
                $(this).toggleClass('menu-active');

                if ($(this).hasClass('menu-active')) {
                    $('.navbar').addClass('bg-blue-transparent');
                } else {
                    $('.navbar').removeClass('bg-blue-transparent');
                }
            });

            $('.mega-menu-item').on('click', function(e) {
                if ($(this).find('ul.stick-menu').length) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    e.stopPropagation();

                    $(this).siblings('.mega-menu-item').removeClass('active');
                    $(this).toggleClass('active');
                } else {
                    e.stopPropagation();
                    $('.mega-menu-item').removeClass('active');
                    $('.nav-item-top').removeClass('menu-active');
                    $('.navbar').removeClass('bg-blue-transparent');
                };
            });

            $('.dropdown-menu a.dropdown-toggle').on('click', function(e) {
                if (!$(this).next().hasClass('show')) {
                    $(this).parents('.dropdown-menu').first().find('.show').removeClass('show');
                }
                var $subMenu = $(this).next('.dropdown-menu');
                $subMenu.toggleClass('show');


                $(this).parents('li.nav-item.dropdown.show').on('hidden.bs.dropdown', function(e) {
                    $('.dropdown-submenu .show').removeClass('show');
                });

                $(this).toggleClass('show');
                return false;
            });
        });
    </script>

    <script>
        // When the user scrolls down 50px from the top of the document, resize the header's font size
        // window.onscroll = function() {
        //     scrollFunction()
        // };

        function scrollFunction() {
            if (document.body.scrollTop > 50 || document.documentElement.scrollTop > 50) {
                document.getElementById("headtop").style.backgroundColor =
                    "linear-gradient(to bottom, black 0%, rgba(0,0,0,0) 100%)";
                document.getElementById("headtop").style.background = "#003D81";
            } else {
                document.getElementById("headtop").style.background = "";
            }
        }
    </script>

        function tampilDetail(id) {
            fetch("https://kudussehat.kuduskab.go.id/api/get-agenda/" + id).then((res) => res.json()).then(result => {
                $("#image_src").attr("src", result.data.gambar);
                $("#url-image").attr("href", result.data.gambar);
                $("#judul").text(result.data.nama);
                $("#desc").html(result.data.des);
            });

    <script>
        let item1 = ""
        let parentTampil = $("#tampil-element")
        $(".item-item").remove()

        kudus.features.forEach(element => {
            if (element.properties.ENGTYPE_3 === "Sub-district") {

                item1 = `<div class="card item-item" style="height: 55px; margin-bottom:5px;cursor: pointer" onclick="showDesa('${element.properties.GID_4}','kecamatan')">
            <div class="card-body">${element.properties.name}</div>
        </div>`
                parentTampil.append(item1)
            }

        })

        function showDesa(gid4, kec) {
            if (kec === "kecamatan") {
                $(".item-item").remove()
            }
            let dataArray1 = []
            kudus.features.forEach(element => {
                if (kec === "kecamatan") {

                    if (element.properties.GID_3 == gid4) {
                        dataArray1.push(element)
                        item = `<div class="card item-item" style="height: 55px; margin-bottom:5px;cursor: pointer" onclick="showDesa('${element.properties.GID_4}','desa')">
                            <div class="card-body">${element.properties.name}</div>
                        </div>`
                        parentTampil.append(item)
                    }
                } else {
                    if (element.properties.GID_4 == gid4) {
                        dataArray1.push(element)
                    }
                }
            });
            let data = {
                "type": "FeatureCollection",
                "features": dataArray1
            }
            map.removeLayer(geoJson)
            drawMap(data)

        }
    </script>
